	local UserInputService = game:GetService("UserInputService")
	local Gui = MainGui
	
	local gui = Gui
	
	local dragging
	local dragInput
	local dragStart
	local startPos
	
	local function update(input)
		local delta = input.Position - dragStart
		gui.Position = UDim2.new(startPos.X.Scale, startPos.X.Offset + delta.X, startPos.Y.Scale, startPos.Y.Offset + delta.Y)
	end
	
	gui.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
		if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
			dragging = true
			dragStart = input.Position
			startPos = gui.Position
	
			input.Changed:Connect(function()
				if input.UserInputState == Enum.UserInputState.End then
					dragging = false
				end
			end)
		end
	end)
	
	gui.InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
		if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
			dragInput = input
		end
	end)
	
	UserInputService.InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
		if input == dragInput and dragging then
			update(input)
		end
	end)

local function frameExists(frameName)
	return Instances:FindFirstChild(frameName) ~= nil
end

				Instances.Messages6.Name="Messages"
			end
		end
	end
end
function ScriptLoad()
	if HttpsGameGet==true then
	TextNotify="Executed."
	ImageID="rbxassetid://9405926389"
	NotifyColor=Color3.new(255, 255, 255)
	Notify()
	if ScriptHubLoad=="Vape" then
		loadstring(game:HttpGet("https://raw.githubusercontent.com/7GrandDadPGN/VapeV4ForRoblox/main/NewMainScript.lua", true))
	elseif ScriptHubLoad=="DomainX" then
		loadstring(game:HttpGet('https://raw.githubusercontent.com/shlexware/DomainX/main/source',true))()
	elseif ScriptHubLoad=="Sirius" then
		loadstring(game:HttpGet('https://sirius.menu/script'))()
	elseif ScriptHubLoad=="ADustyTrip" then
		loadstring(game:HttpGet("https://raw.githubusercontent.com/artemy133563/Utilities/main/ADustyTrip",true))()
	elseif ScriptHubLoad=="ADMINUS Devil Fruit Sniper V2" then
		loadstring(game:HttpGet("https://raw.githubusercontent.com/flerci42/Adminus_FruitSniper_V2/main/.lua", true))()
	elseif ScriptHubLoad=="AlphaXHub" then
		loadstring(game:HttpGet('https://raw.githubusercontent.com/zAlpha07/Loader-Main-/main/AlphaXHubWorking.Lua'))()
	elseif ScriptHubLoad=="Primordial" then
		loadstring(game:HttpGet("https://raw.githubusercontent.com/Bovanlaarhoven/Primordial/main/src/loader.lua"))()
	elseif ScriptHubLoad=="InfiniteYield" then
		loadstring(game:HttpGet('https://raw.githubusercontent.com/EdgeIY/infiniteyield/master/source'))()
	elseif ScriptHubLoad=="MySploit" then
		loadstring(game:HttpGet("https://raw.githubusercontent.com/wuhaz/MySploit/main/Arsenal.lua"))()
    elseif ScriptHubLoad=="NinjaLegendsOP" then--key
		loadstring(game:HttpGet("https://raw.githubusercontent.com/ImPocky/PockyHub/main/Scripts/load.txt"))()
	elseif ScriptHubLoad=="DarkHubV2" then
		loadstring(game:HttpGet("https://raw.githubusercontent.com/D8rkX/D8rk-Hub/main/Games/Evade.lua",true))()
	elseif ScriptHubLoad=="MurderMysteryV2" then
		loadstring(game:HttpGet("https://raw.githubusercontent.com/Pa1nx/MurderMystery2ScriptTESTING/main/TestFile"))()
	elseif ScriptHubLoad=="PrisonLife" then
		loadstring(game:HttpGet("https://raw.githubusercontent.com/tbao143/thaibao/main/TbaohubPrisonLife"))()
	elseif ScriptHubLoad=="TowerOfHell" then
			loadstring(game:HttpGet("https://raw.githubusercontent.com/SpedCoding/Delta-Hub/main/Framework"))()
	elseif ScriptHubLoad=="BuildAboatAutoFarm" then
		loadstring(game:HttpGet('https://raw.githubusercontent.com/1201for/V.G-Hub/main/V.Ghub'))()
	elseif ScriptHubLoad=="DeathBall" then
		loadstring(game:HttpGet("https://raw.githubusercontent.com/sirapobsriumang/Death-Bal/main/Op-Script-by-me"))()
	elseif ScriptHubLoad=="NamelessAdmin" then
		loadstring(game:HttpGet("https://raw.githubusercontent.com/FilteringEnabled/NamelessAdmin/main/Source"))();
	--elseif ScriptHubLoad=="" then
		
	else
		warn("no script to ran probably error with executor report to dev!")
		end
	elseif HttpsGameGet==false then
		TextNotify="Cannot execute in studio"
		ImageID="rbxassetid://12988744896"
		NotifyColor=Color3.new(1, 0.584314, 0.223529)
		Notify()
	end
end

if AutoUpdater==true then
	TextNotify="Updated!"
	ImageID="rbxassetid://9405926389"
	NotifyColor=Color3.new(255, 255, 255)
	NotifyTime = 5.3
	Notify()

local inputMenu = Enum.KeyCode.End
local inputMenuActive = true--menu shortcut
local userInputService = game:GetService("UserInputService")

userInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gameProccesedEvent)
	if input.KeyCode == inputMenu then
		if inputMenuActive==true then
			if userInputService:GetFocusedTextBox() ~= nil then return end
			if GuiHidden == false then
				game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(TransparencyValue1,TweenInfo.new(0.1,Enum.EasingStyle.Linear),{BackgroundTransparency = 1}):Play()
				game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(TextTransparencyValue1,TweenInfo.new(0.1,Enum.EasingStyle.Linear),{BackgroundTransparency = 1}):Play()
				game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(ImageTransparencyValue1,TweenInfo.new(0.1,Enum.EasingStyle.Linear),{BackgroundTransparency = 1}):Play()
				MainGui.ScriptFrame.Visible = false
				game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(MainGui.Buttons.Button1Background,TweenInfo.new(0.1,Enum.EasingStyle.Linear),{BackgroundTransparency = 1}):Play()
				game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(MainGui.Buttons.Button2Background,TweenInfo.new(0.1,Enum.EasingStyle.Linear),{BackgroundTransparency = 1}):Play()
				game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(MainGui.Buttons.Button3Background,TweenInfo.new(0.1,Enum.EasingStyle.Linear),{BackgroundTransparency = 1}):Play()
				game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(MainGui.Buttons.Button4Background,TweenInfo.new(0.1,Enum.EasingStyle.Linear),{BackgroundTransparency = 1}):Play()
				game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(MainGui.Buttons.Button1Background.Button1,TweenInfo.new(0.1,Enum.EasingStyle.Linear),{ImageTransparency = 1}):Play()
				game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(MainGui.Buttons.Button1Background.UIStroke,TweenInfo.new(0.1,Enum.EasingStyle.Linear),{Transparency = 1}):Play()
				game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(MainGui.Buttons.Button2Background.Button2,TweenInfo.new(0.1,Enum.EasingStyle.Linear),{ImageTransparency = 1}):Play()
				game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(MainGui.Buttons.Button2Background.UIStroke,TweenInfo.new(0.1,Enum.EasingStyle.Linear),{Transparency = 1}):Play()
				game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(MainGui.Buttons.Button3Background.Button3,TweenInfo.new(0.1,Enum.EasingStyle.Linear),{ImageTransparency = 1}):Play()
				game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(MainGui.Buttons.Button3Background.UIStroke,TweenInfo.new(0.1,Enum.EasingStyle.Linear),{Transparency = 1}):Play()
				game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(MainGui.Buttons.Button4Background.Button4,TweenInfo.new(0.1,Enum.EasingStyle.Linear),{ImageTransparency = 1}):Play()
				game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(MainGui.Buttons.Button4Background.UIStroke,TweenInfo.new(0.1,Enum.EasingStyle.Linear),{Transparency = 1}):Play()
				game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(MainGui.ImageLabel,TweenInfo.new(0.1,Enum.EasingStyle.Linear),{ImageTransparency = 1}):Play()
				AsuraX.ScrollingFrame.Visible=false
				AsuraX.ScrollingFrame_2.Visible=false
				MainGui:TweenSize(
					UDim2.new(0, 641,0, 25),
					"Out",
					"Quad",
					0.3,
					false
				)
				game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(MainGui.Icons.CloseButton,TweenInfo.new(0.3,Enum.EasingStyle.Linear),{ImageTransparency = 1}):Play()
				game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(MainGui.Icons.HideButton,TweenInfo.new(0.3,Enum.EasingStyle.Linear),{ImageTransparency = 1}):Play()
				wait(0.3)
				game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(MainGui.UIStroke,TweenInfo.new(0.1,Enum.EasingStyle.Linear),{Transparency = 1}):Play()
				game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(MainGui,TweenInfo.new(0.1,Enum.EasingStyle.Linear),{BackgroundTransparency = 1}):Play()
				wait(0.2)
				MainGui.Visible = false
				GuiHidden=true
			else
				MainGui.Visible = true
				MainGui:TweenSize(
					UDim2.new(0, 641,0, 379),
					"Out",
					"Quad",
					0.3,
					false
				)
				AsuraX.ScrollingFrame.Visible=true
				AsuraX.ScrollingFrame_2.Visible=true
				game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(MainGui.Icons.CloseButton,TweenInfo.new(0.3,Enum.EasingStyle.Linear),{ImageTransparency = 0.4}):Play()
				game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(MainGui.Icons.HideButton,TweenInfo.new(0.3,Enum.EasingStyle.Linear),{ImageTransparency = 0.4}):Play()
				wait(0.3)
				game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(MainGui.UIStroke,TweenInfo.new(0.1,Enum.EasingStyle.Linear),{Transparency = 0}):Play()
				game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(MainGui,TweenInfo.new(0.1,Enum.EasingStyle.Linear),{BackgroundTransparency = 0}):Play()
				wait(0.2)
				game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(MainGui.ImageLabel,TweenInfo.new(0.1,Enum.EasingStyle.Linear),{ImageTransparency = 0}):Play() 
				if Button1List==true then
					game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(MainGui.Buttons.Button1Background,TweenInfo.new(0.1,Enum.EasingStyle.Linear),{BackgroundTransparency = 0}):Play()
					game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(MainGui.Buttons.Button1Background.Button1,TweenInfo.new(0.1,Enum.EasingStyle.Linear),{ImageTransparency = 0.46}):Play()
					game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(MainGui.Buttons.Button1Background.UIStroke,TweenInfo.new(0.1,Enum.EasingStyle.Linear),{Transparency = 0}):Play()

					game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(MainGui.Buttons.Button3Background.UIStroke,TweenInfo.new(0.1,Enum.EasingStyle.Linear),{Transparency = 1}):Play()
					game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(MainGui.Buttons.Button4Background,TweenInfo.new(0.1,Enum.EasingStyle.Linear),{BackgroundTransparency = 0}):Play()
					game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(MainGui.Buttons.Button4Background.Button4,TweenInfo.new(0.1,Enum.EasingStyle.Linear),{ImageTransparency = 0.46}):Play()
					game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(MainGui.Buttons.Button4Background.UIStroke,TweenInfo.new(0.1,Enum.EasingStyle.Linear),{Transparency = 0}):Play()
				end
				warn("ran")
				if HideName=="ExecutorFrame" then
					game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(TransparencyValue1,TweenInfo.new(0.1,Enum.EasingStyle.Linear),{BackgroundTransparency = 0}):Play()
					game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(TextTransparencyValue1,TweenInfo.new(0.1,Enum.EasingStyle.Linear),{BackgroundTransparency = 0.6}):Play()
					game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(ImageTransparencyValue1,TweenInfo.new(0.1,Enum.EasingStyle.Linear),{BackgroundTransparency = 0.2}):Play()
				elseif HideName=="ScriptFrame" then
					MainGui.ScriptFrame.Visible = true
				end
				GuiHidden=false
			end
		end
	end
end)
local Tab1 = true
local Tab2 = false
local Tab3 = false
local Tab4 = false
local Tab5 = false
local Tab6 = false
local Tab7 = false


function AddTab()
	
end

	while true do
		wait(0.1)
		--warn("tabnumber  "..TabNumber,"Text1"..Editor1Text,"Text2"..Editor2Text)
		MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ListGui.ADDTabFrame.ADDTab.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		if TabNumber==1 then
			Editor1Text=MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ExecutorFrame.Frame.ScrollingFrame.TextBox.Text
		end
		TabNumber = TabNumber + 1
			TabOpen = TabOpen + 1
			if TabNumber==2 then
			Editor2Text=MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ExecutorFrame.Frame.ScrollingFrame.TextBox.Text
			elseif  TabNumber==3 then
				Editor3Text=MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ExecutorFrame.Frame.ScrollingFrame.TextBox.Text
			end
			--print("numberoftab"..TabNumber)
		MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ListGui.ADDTabFrame:Destroy()
		Instances["Editor#"]:Clone().Parent = MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ListGui
		MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ListGui["Editor#"].Visible = true
		Instances.ADDTabFrame:Clone().Parent = MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ListGui
		MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ListGui["Editor#"].TextButton.Text = "Editor #"..TabNumber
		MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ListGui["Editor#"].Name = "Editor#"..TabNumber
		MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ListGui.ADDTabFrame.Visible=true
		MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ExecutorFrame.Frame.ScrollingFrame.TextBox.Text="Editor2Text"
		end)
		MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ListGui["Editor#"..TabNumber].RemoveIcon.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ListGui["Editor#"..TabNumber]:Destroy()
			if TabNumber==1 then
				MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ExecutorFrame.Frame.ScrollingFrame.TextBox.Text=""..Editor1Text
			elseif TabNumber==2 then
				MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ExecutorFrame.Frame.ScrollingFrame.TextBox.Text=""..Editor2Text
			elseif TabNumber==3 then
				Editor3Text=MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ExecutorFrame.Frame.ScrollingFrame.TextBox.Text
			elseif TabNumber==4 then
				MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ExecutorFrame.Frame.ScrollingFrame.TextBox.Text=Editor4Text
				Editor4Text=MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ExecutorFrame.Frame.ScrollingFrame.TextBox.Text
			elseif TabNumber==5 then
				MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ExecutorFrame.Frame.ScrollingFrame.TextBox.Text=Editor5Text
				Editor5Text=MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ExecutorFrame.Frame.ScrollingFrame.TextBox.Text
			elseif TabNumber==6 then
				MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ExecutorFrame.Frame.ScrollingFrame.TextBox.Text=Editor6Text
				Editor6Text=MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ExecutorFrame.Frame.ScrollingFrame.TextBox.Text
			elseif TabNumber==7 then
				MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ExecutorFrame.Frame.ScrollingFrame.TextBox.Text=Editor7Text
				Editor7Text=MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ExecutorFrame.Frame.ScrollingFrame.TextBox.Text
			end
			TabNumber = TabNumber - 1
		end)
	--[[	MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ListGui["Editor#"..TabNumber].TextButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			if TabNumber==2 then
				MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ExecutorFrame.Frame.ScrollingFrame.TextBox.Text=""..Editor2Text
			elseif TabNumber==3 then
				Editor3Text=MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ExecutorFrame.Frame.ScrollingFrame.TextBox.Text
			elseif TabNumber==4 then
				MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ExecutorFrame.Frame.ScrollingFrame.TextBox.Text=Editor4Text
				Editor4Text=MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ExecutorFrame.Frame.ScrollingFrame.TextBox.Text
			elseif TabNumber==5 then
				MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ExecutorFrame.Frame.ScrollingFrame.TextBox.Text=Editor5Text
				Editor5Text=MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ExecutorFrame.Frame.ScrollingFrame.TextBox.Text
			elseif TabNumber==6 then
				MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ExecutorFrame.Frame.ScrollingFrame.TextBox.Text=Editor6Text
				Editor6Text=MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ExecutorFrame.Frame.ScrollingFrame.TextBox.Text
			elseif TabNumber==7 then
				MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ExecutorFrame.Frame.ScrollingFrame.TextBox.Text=Editor7Text
				Editor7Text=MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ExecutorFrame.Frame.ScrollingFrame.TextBox.Text
			end
		end)--]]
		MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ListGui["Editor#1"].TextButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			Editor2Text=MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ExecutorFrame.Frame.ScrollingFrame.TextBox.Text
			wait(0.1)
			MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ExecutorFrame.Frame.ScrollingFrame.TextBox.Text=""..Editor1Text
			TabOpen=1
		end)
	MainGui.ExecutorFrame.DownGui.BackgroundTransparency = TransparencyValue1.BackgroundTransparency
	MainGui.ExecutorFrame.BackgroundTransparency = TransparencyValue1.BackgroundTransparency
	MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ExecutorFrameSide.BackgroundTransparency = TransparencyValue1.BackgroundTransparency
	MainGui.ExecutorFrame.DownGui.AttachFrame.BackgroundTransparency = TransparencyValue1.BackgroundTransparency
	MainGui.ExecutorFrame.DownGui.ClearFrame.BackgroundTransparency = TransparencyValue1.BackgroundTransparency
	MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ExecutorFrame.BackgroundTransparency = TransparencyValue1.BackgroundTransparency
	MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ExecutorFrame.Frame.BackgroundTransparency = TransparencyValue1.BackgroundTransparency
	MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ExecutorFrame.Frame.ScrollingFrame.TextBox.TextTransparency = TransparencyValue1.BackgroundTransparency
	MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ListGui.ADDTabFrame.ADDTab.ImageTransparency = ImageTransparencyValue1.BackgroundTransparency
	MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ListGui["Editor#1"].BackgroundTransparency = TransparencyValue1.BackgroundTransparency
	MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ListGui["Editor#1"].TextButton.TextTransparency = TransparencyValue1.BackgroundTransparency
	MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ListGui["Editor#1"].RemoveIcon.ImageTransparency = ImageTransparencyValue1.BackgroundTransparency
	MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ListGui["Editor#2"].BackgroundTransparency = TransparencyValue1.BackgroundTransparency
	MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ListGui["Editor#2"].TextButton.TextTransparency = TransparencyValue1.BackgroundTransparency
	MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ListGui["Editor#2"].RemoveIcon.ImageTransparency = ImageTransparencyValue1.BackgroundTransparency
	MainGui.ExecutorFrame.DownGui.ExecuteFrame.BackgroundTransparency = TransparencyValue1.BackgroundTransparency
	MainGui.ExecutorFrame.DownGui.ExecuteFrame.ImageButton.ImageTransparency = TextTransparencyValue1.BackgroundTransparency
	MainGui.ExecutorFrame.DownGui.AttachFrame.ImageButton.ImageTransparency = TextTransparencyValue1.BackgroundTransparency
	MainGui.ExecutorFrame.DownGui.ClearFrame.ImageButton.ImageTransparency = TextTransparencyValue1.BackgroundTransparency
	MainGui.ExecutorFrame.DownGui.AttachFrame.UIStroke.Transparency = TransparencyValue1.BackgroundTransparency
	MainGui.ExecutorFrame.DownGui.ClearFrame.UIStroke.Transparency = TransparencyValue1.BackgroundTransparency
	MainGui.ExecutorFrame.DownGui.ExecuteFrame.UIStroke.Transparency = TransparencyValue1.BackgroundTransparency
	if Tab2==true then
		MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ListGui["Editor#2"].TextButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			Editor2Text=MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ExecutorFrame.Frame.ScrollingFrame.TextBox.Text
			wait(0.1)
			MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ExecutorFrame.Frame.ScrollingFrame.TextBox.Text=""..Editor2Text
			TabOpen=2
		end)
	end
	if Tab3==true then
		MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ListGui["Editor#3"].TextButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			Editor3Text=MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ExecutorFrame.Frame.ScrollingFrame.TextBox.Text
			wait(0.1)
			MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ExecutorFrame.Frame.ScrollingFrame.TextBox.Text=""..Editor3Text
			TabOpen=3
		end)
	end
	if Tab4==true then
		MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ListGui["Editor#4"].TextButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			Editor4Text=MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ExecutorFrame.Frame.ScrollingFrame.TextBox.Text
			wait(0.1)
			MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ExecutorFrame.Frame.ScrollingFrame.TextBox.Text=""..Editor4Text
			TabOpen=4
		end)
	end
	if Tab5==true then
		MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ListGui["Editor#5"].TextButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
			Editor5Text=MainGui.ExecutorFrame.ExecutorFrame.Frame.ScrollingFrame.TextBox.Text
			wait(0.1)

	if Tab6==true then

			wait(0.1)
